\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00154}00154 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Womersley (parallel flow) equations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00155}00155 \textcolor{comment}{  /// \(\backslash\)f[ Re St \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial u\}\{\(\backslash\)partial t\} = -\/ g + \(\backslash\)frac\{\(\backslash\)partial\string^2 u\}\{\(\backslash\)partial x\_i\string^2\} \(\backslash\)f]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00156}00156 \textcolor{comment}{  /// which may be derived from the full Navier-\/Stokes equations}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00157}00157 \textcolor{comment}{  /// (with a viscous scaling of the pressure) under the assumption of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00158}00158 \textcolor{comment}{  /// parallel flow in the z direction. u then represents the axial}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00159}00159 \textcolor{comment}{  /// velocity and g is the (spatially constant) axial component of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00160}00160 \textcolor{comment}{  /// the pressure gradient.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00161}00161 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00162}00162 \textcolor{comment}{  /// This class contains the generic maths. Shape functions, geometric}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00163}00163 \textcolor{comment}{  /// mapping etc. must get implemented in derived class.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00164}00164 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Note that this class assumes an isoparametric formulation, i.e. that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00165}00165 \textcolor{comment}{  /// the scalar unknown is interpolated using the same shape functions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00166}00166 \textcolor{comment}{  /// as the position.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00167}00167 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00168}00168 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Generally, the instantaneous value of the pressure gradient, g,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00169}00169 \textcolor{comment}{  /// is prescribed (and specified via a pointer to a single-\/valued}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00170}00170 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Data object whose current (pinned) value contains the pressure.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00171}00171 \textcolor{comment}{  ///}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00172}00172 \textcolor{comment}{  /// It is also possible to prescribe the flow rate through}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00173}00173 \textcolor{comment}{  /// a mesh of Womersley elements and to determine the pressure}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00174}00174 \textcolor{comment}{  /// gradient required to achieve this flow rate as an unknown.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00175}00175 \textcolor{comment}{  /// In that case the external pressure is treated as}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00176}00176 \textcolor{comment}{  /// an external Data object that an associated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00177}00177 \textcolor{comment}{  /// ImposeFluxForWomersleyElement is in charge of. Note that only}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00178}00178 \textcolor{comment}{  /// the ImposeFluxForWomersleyElement can set the pressure gradient}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00179}00179 \textcolor{comment}{  /// Data object as external Data. This is because (counter to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00180}00180 \textcolor{comment}{  /// general practice) the WomersleyEquations make contributions}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00181}00181 \textcolor{comment}{  /// to the residuals of the ImposeFluxForWomersleyElements in order}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00182}00182 \textcolor{comment}{  /// to keep the elemental Jacobians as small as possible.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l00183}00183 \textcolor{comment}{}  \textcolor{comment}{//=============================================================}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l02718}02718   \textcolor{comment}{//======================================================================}\textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l02719}02719 \textcolor{comment}{  /// A class for an element to control net fluid flux across a boundary}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l02720}02720 \textcolor{comment}{  /// by imposing an applied pressure to the Navier-\/Stokes equations.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l02721}02721 \textcolor{comment}{  /// This element is used with a mesh of NavierStokesFluxControlElements}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l02722}02722 \textcolor{comment}{  /// attached to the boundary. The flux imposed by this element is given}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{womersley__elements_8h_source_l02723}02723 \textcolor{comment}{  /// by a NavierStokesWomersleyPressureControlElement.}}
